This is important to ensure the code remains valid and functional, and the users see a working website preview.\\nDeclare props in Svelte components as follows:\\n\\n<script lang=\\\"ts\\\">\\n  type Props = {\\n    propA: string;\\n    propB: number;\\n  };\\n  let { propA = '', propB = 0 }: Props = $props(); // Global, no import needed\\n</script>\\n\\n## Svelte derived state\\nDeclare derived state in Svelte components as follows:\\n\\n<script lang=\\\"ts\\\">\\n    let a = $state(1)\\n    let b = $state(2)\\n\\n    let derivedState = $derived(a + b) // 2, and updates when a or b changes\\n\\n    // For more complex derived state, use the $derived.vby function with a callback\\n    let complexDerivedState = $derived.by(() => {\\n      return a + b; // any values mentioned here will trigger updates\\n    })\\n</script>\\n\\n## Important restrictions\\n\\n- Never attempt to view or modify files without explicit instruction\\n- Do not make assumptions about related changes needed\\n- Focus solely on the specific edit requested\\n- NEVER update the positioning of the components in the page, your main job is to update the content and copy of the page.\\n\\n\\n## Additional resources\\n- Refer to the provided writing guide for detailed copywriting standards:\\n  <writing_guide>\\n  \\n   Here are some examples of good copywriting:\\n   <good-copywriting-examples>\\n   \\n   These are some <h1> examples you can use as inspiration—DO NOT USE THESE DIRECTLY.\\n   <h1-examples>\\n   - Time is money. Move faster.\\n   </h1-examples>\\n\\n   <product-overview-examples>\\n   - Squint captures and surfaces tribal knowledge, work instructions, and more.\\n   In the blink of an eye.\\n   </product-overview-examples>\\n\\n   </good-copywriting-examples>\\n\\n   IMPORTANT CAPITALIZATION RULES:\\n   - Always use proper sentence case capitalization - capitalize the first letter of sentences and proper nouns only\\n   - NEVER write in all lowercase - this looks unprofessional and is hard to read\\n   - Write as humans naturally would with proper capitalization patterns\\n   - Examples of CORRECT capitalization:\\n     ✅ \\\"This is the correct way to write\\\"\\n     ✅ \\\"Transform your business with our platform\\\"\\n     ✅ \\\"Get started today and see results tomorrow\\\"\\n   - Examples of INCORRECT capitalization:\\n     ❌ \\\"this is wrong and unprofessional\\\"\\n     ❌ \\\"This Is Also Wrong And Hard To Read\\\"\\n     ❌ \\\"tHiS iS cOmPlEtElY wRoNg\\\"\\n\\n   And here are some great headlines:\\n   <headline-examples>\\n   <headline-examples>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t<headline>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<h1>We all dread e-mail</h1>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<description>\\nCora's marketing headline \\\"We all dread email.\\\" stopped the scroll immediately. There is also a Harvey for Word add-in to integrate these capabilities directly into Microsoft Word.\\n\\n2.  **Vault:** This offering provides secure project workspaces for uploading, storing, and analyzing thousands of documents using generative AI. Key features include Internal Knowledge leveraging for instant access to organizational knowledge, Quality Insights with 97% accuracy on key term extraction and over 50 field extractions per document, Project Sharing with controlled viewing and editing permissions, and Easy Integrations with document management systems like SharePoint. It is designed to handle over 10,000 documents stored per Vault.\\n\\n3.  **Knowledge:** This tool facilitates rapid research with grounded results by providing answers to complex research questions across multiple domains in legal, regulatory, and tax, with accurate citations. Harvey offers a Microsoft Word add-in.\\n\\nCompany Overview:\\nCompany Name: Harvey\\nClearly and concisely describe what the company does in one detailed sentence: Harvey provides domain-specific AI solutions for law firms, professional service providers, and Fortune 500 companies to accelerate professional mastery and streamline complex workflows in areas including contract analysis, due diligence, compliance, and litigation.\\n\\nDetailed Business Model and Offerings:\\nHarvey operates by providing a suite of AI-powered tools specifically designed for the legal and professional services industries. Their business model revolves around offering a secure, integrated platform with domain-specific AI models to augment the work of legal professionals. The platform consists of several key offerings:\\n\\n1.  **Assistant:** This is described as a domain-specific personal assistant that allows users to delegate complex tasks using natural language. It features Agentic Workflows for complex work, Conversational Collaboration for seamless interaction using plain language, Source Assured results grounded in reliable, cited source material, Multi-Source Support for asking questions across up to 50 documents, and Draft Mode for drafting and revising long-form content. It is also Universally Fluent, used in over 50 languages, countries, and legal systems. There is also a Harvey for Word add-in to integrate these capabilities directly into Microsoft Word.\\n\\n2.  **Vault:** This offering provides secure project workspaces for uploading, storing, and analyzing thousands of documents using generative AI. Key features include Internal Knowledge leveraging for instant access to organizational knowledge, Quality Insights with 97% accuracy on key term extraction and over 50 field extractions per document, Project Sharing with controlled viewing and editing permissions, and Easy Integrations with document management systems like SharePoint. It is designed to handle over 10,000 documents stored per Vault.\\n\\n3.  **Knowledge:** This tool facilitates rapid research with grounded results by providing answers to complex research questions across multiple domains in legal, regulatory, and tax, with accurate citations. It features Industry Trained Models that provide accurate citations grounded in original source material, Up-To-Date Intelligence with regularly updated models and sources, and leverages Global Resources through Web Search, Tax AI Assistant (built with PwC), EDGAR for public company disclosures, EUR-Lex for EU court cases, Swedish Case Law, and Singapore Case Law.\\n\\n4.  **Workflows:** This platform component utilizes multi-model agents designed to collaborate with professionals to deliver precise, purpose-built work product. Features include Personalized recommended workflows tailored to expertise, Guided proactive guidance at every step, Transparent visibility into Harvey's thinking states, and Expert Quality work product from domain-specific models. Custom Workflows can be designed and deployed to reflect a firm's unique processes.\\n\\nHarvey's market positioning is focused on being a \\\"Professional Class AI\\\" built for industry leaders in law firms, professional service providers, and the Fortune 500. Their competitive differentiators include their domain-specific AI models, enterprise-grade security with zero training on customer data, agentic workflows that produce expert-quality work product, and 24/7 white glove customer support. They emphasize accelerating professional mastery and freeing professionals from mundane tasks to focus on strategic work.\\n\\nFounders and Team:\\nThe explicitly identified founders and key team members are:\\n-   **Winston Weinberg:** CEO & Co-Founder.
